[09/01/23, 4:03:45â€¯PM] Gaurav Rao: As observed during the recent visit at the many outlets, there is a considerable increase in the visibility of the signage, and the burger@39 signage is only visible during the day when the signage is turned on.

Considering the same we have revised signage related protocol as follows:
All indoor signage/logo:  Mandatory "Switch ON" throughout the operational hour.
"BURGER @ 39" signage:  Mandatory  "Switch ON" throughout the operational hour  
Main Signage / Outdoor lollipop / Logo (excluding burger@39)
Till 5 pm:  Our recommendation will be to keep it switched on throughout operational hours if it adds any further visibility. 
5 pm Onwards (till the store is operational):  Mandatory "Switch ON"

Going forward the same will also be incorporated into the restaurant audit.
